2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eFrom the readme, there's a main invariant -\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cblockquote\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eUsers that deposit ETH/WETH get the correct amount of lpETH on claim (1 to 1 conversion)\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/blockquote\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThis 1 to 1 invariant can be easily broken through donations, before the \u003ccode\u003econvertAllETH\u003c/code\u003e function is called. The function queries the balance of ETH before conerting all to lpETH, and queries the contract's lpETH balance to set the \u003ccode\u003etotalLpETH\u003c/code\u003e parameter. The conversion rate is 1 to 1.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-solidity notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"    function convertAllETH() external onlyAuthorized onlyBeforeDate(startClaimDate) {\n        if (block.timestamp - loopActivation \u0026lt;= TIMELOCK) {\n            revert LoopNotActivated();\n        }\n\n        // deposits all the ETH to lpETH contract. Receives lpETH back\n        uint256 totalBalance = address(this).balance;\n        lpETH.deposit{value: totalBalance}(address(this));\n\n        totalLpETH = lpETH.balanceOf(address(this));\n\n        // Claims of lpETH can start immediately after conversion.\n        startClaimDate = uint32(block.timestamp);\n\n        emit Converted(totalBalance, totalLpETH);\n    }\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e    \u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003efunction\u003cspan class=\"pl-en\"\u003e convertAllETH\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e() \u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003eexternal\u003c/span\u003e onlyAuthorized \u003cspan class=\"pl-en\"\u003eonlyBeforeDate\u003c/span\u003e(startClaimDate) {\n        \u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003eif\u003c/span\u003e (\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003eblock\u003c/span\u003e.\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003etimestamp\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003e-\u003c/span\u003e loopActivation \u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003e\u0026lt;=\u003c/span\u003e TIMELOCK) {\n            \u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003erevert\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-en\"\u003eLoopNotActivated\u003c/span\u003e();\n        }\n\n        \u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e// deposits all the ETH to lpETH contract. So if tokens had been donated, they'll be converted to \u003ccode\u003elpETH\u003c/code\u003e without actually changing the totalSupply.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eWhen claiming, the claimed amount a user is entitled to is calculated as \u003ccode\u003euserStake\u003c/code\u003e * \u003ccode\u003etotalLpETH\u003c/code\u003e/\u003ccode\u003etotalSupply\u003c/code\u003e. And as it has been established that \u003ccode\u003etotalLpETH\u003c/code\u003e was a 1 to 1 exchange, this means that it will be more than \u003ccode\u003etotalSupply\u003c/code\u003e (since donations had increased \u003ccode\u003eaddress(this).balance\u003c/code\u003e but didn't affect \u003ccode\u003etotalSupply\u003c/code\u003e). As \u003ccode\u003etotalLpETH\u003c/code\u003e is more than \u003ccode\u003etotalSupply\u003c/code\u003e, a user's claimed amount will not be in a 1 to 1 ratio with his staked amount, but rather more.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-solidity notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"    function _claim(address _token, address _receiver, uint8 _percentage, Exchange _exchange, bytes calldata _data)\n        internal\n        returns (uint256 claimedAmount)\n    {\n        uint256 userStake = balances[msg.sender][_token];\n        if (userStake == 0) {\n            revert NothingToClaim();\n        }\n        if (_token == ETH) {\n            claimedAmount = userStake.mulDiv(totalLpETH, totalSupply);\n            balances[msg.sender][_token] = 0;\n            lpETH.safeTransfer(_receiver, claimedAmount);\n        }\n        ...\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e    \u003cspan balances[\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003emsg\u003c/span\u003e.\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003esender\u003c/span\u003e][_token];\n        \u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003eif\u003c/span\u003e (userStake 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eDepending on how much amount a user had staked, and how much percentage they're willing to claim, users might not be able to claim any token due to precision loss, due to the product of \u003ccode\u003euserStake\u003c/code\u003e and \u003ccode\u003e_percentage\u003c/code\u003e being smaller than 100. This is mostly for users with smaller stakes which will not be uncommon, due to the prices of LSTs. Consider scaling up the percentages to handle this potential precision loss.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-solidity notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"        if (_token == ETH) {\n            claimedAmount = userStake.mulDiv(totalLpETH, totalSupply);\n            balances[msg.sender][_token] = 0;\n            lpETH.safeTransfer(_receiver, claimedAmount);\n        } else {\n            uint256 userClaim = userStake * _percentage / 100;\n            _validateData(_token, userClaim, _exchange, _data);\n            balances[msg.sender][_token] = userStake - contract's \u003ccode\u003eETH\u003c/code\u003e has been completely converted to lpETH, their respective values are tracked with \u003ccode\u003etotalSupply\u003c/code\u003e and \u003ccode\u003etotalLpETH\u003c/code\u003e parameters. Since these cannot be changed any longer after \u003ccode\u003estartClaimDate\u003c/code\u003e, their values can be used, to determine if excess \u003ccode\u003eETH\u003c/code\u003e and \u003ccode\u003elpETH\u003c/code\u003e have been sent to the contract, and can be used to retrieve them without disturbing the contracts internal accounting. class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">1. Tokens cannot be disallowed</h2><a id="user-content-1-tokens-cannot-be-disallowed" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 1. <div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Impact</h3><a id="user-content-impact" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Impact" href="#impact"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Tokens can be allowed but cannot be disallowed. In case of an admin error, and the wrong token being allowed, there's no way for this to be rectified. In cases of depeg or blackswan, slashing events, worthless tokens will be exchangable for <code>lpETH</code>.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-solidity notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="    function allowToken(address _token) external onlyAuthorized {
        isTokenAllowed[_token] = true;
    }"><pre>    <span class="pl-k">function<span class="pl-en"> allowToken</span></span>(<span class="pl-c1">address</span> <span class="pl-v">_token</span>) <span class="pl-k">external</span> onlyAuthorized {
        isTokenAllowed[_token] <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">true</span>;
    }</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Recommended Mitigation Steps</h3><a id="user-content-recommended-mitigation-steps" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Recommended Mitigation Steps" href="#recommended-mitigation-steps"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Consider introducing a function to disallow tokens.</p>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">2. Users being able to donate to <code>ETH</code> or <code>lpETH</code> before conversion one of protocol's main invariant</h2><a id="user-content-2-users-being-able-to-donate-to-eth-or-lpeth-before-conversion-one-of-protocols-main-invariant" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 2. Users being able to donate to ETH or lpETH before conversion one of protocol's main invariant" href="#2-users-being-able-to-donate-to-eth-or-lpeth-before-conversion-one-of-protocols-main-invariant"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Links to affected code *</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/code-423n4/2024-05-loop/blob/0dc8467ccff27230e7c0530b619524cc8401e22a/src/PrelaunchPoints.sol#L392">https://github.com/code-423n4/2024-05-loop/blob/0dc8467ccff27230e7c0530b619524cc8401e22a/src/PrelaunchPoints.sol#L392</a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Impact</h3><a id="user-content-impact-1" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Impact" href="#impact-1"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">From the readme, there's a main invariant -</p>
<blockquote>
<p dir="auto">Users that deposit ETH/WETH get the correct amount of lpETH on claim (1 to 1 conversion)</p>
</blockquote>
<p dir="auto">This 1 to 1 invariant can be easily broken through donations, before the <code>convertAllETH</code> function is called. The function queries the balance of ETH before conerting all to lpETH, and queries the contract's lpETH balance to set the <code>totalLpETH</code> parameter. The conversion rate is 1 to 1.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-solidity notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="    function convertAllETH() external onlyAuthorized onlyBeforeDate(startClaimDate) {
        if (block.timestamp - loopActivation &lt;= TIMELOCK) {
            revert LoopNotActivated();
        }

        // deposits all the ETH to lpETH contract. Receives lpETH back
        uint256 totalBalance = address(this).balance;
        lpETH.deposit{value: totalBalance}(address(this));

        totalLpETH = lpETH.balanceOf(address(this));

        // Claims of lpETH can start immediately after conversion.
        startClaimDate = uint32(block.timestamp);

        emit Converted(totalBalance, totalLpETH);
    }"><pre>    <span class="pl-k">function<span class="pl-en"> convertAllETH</span></span>() <span class="pl-k">external</span> onlyAuthorized <span class="pl-en">onlyBeforeDate</span>(startClaimDate) {
        <span class="pl-k">if</span> (<span class="pl-c1">block</span>.<span class="pl-c1">timestamp</span> <span class="pl-k">-</span> loopActivation <span class="pl-k">&lt;=</span> TIMELOCK) {
            <span class="pl-k">revert</span> <span class="pl-en">LoopNotActivated</span>();
        }

        <span class="pl-c">// deposits all the ETH to lpETH contract. Receives lpETH back</span>
        <span class="pl-c1">uint256</span> totalBalance <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">address</span>(<span class="pl-mi">this</span>).balance;
        lpETH.<span class="pl-en">deposit</span>{value: totalBalance}(<span class="pl-c1">address</span>(<span class="pl-mi">this</span>));

        totalLpETH <span class="pl-k">=</span> lpETH.<span class="pl-en">balanceOf</span>(<span class="pl-c1">address</span>(<span class="pl-mi">this</span>));

        <span class="pl-c">// Claims of lpETH can start immediately after conversion.</span>
        startClaimDate <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">uint32</span>(<span class="pl-c1">block</span>.<span class="pl-c1">timestamp</span>);

        <span class="pl-k">emit</span> <span class="pl-en">Converted</span>(totalBalance, totalLpETH);
    }</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Note the <code>totalSupply</code> tracks <code>ETH</code> deposits only through the <a href="https://github.com/code-423n4/2024-05-loop/blob/40167e469edde09969643b6808c57e25d1b9c203/src/PrelaunchPoints.sol#L180-L181"><code>_processLock</code></a> function, meaning it isn't affected by donations. So if tokens had been donated, they'll be converted to <code>lpETH</code> without actually changing the totalSupply.</p>
<p dir="auto">When claiming, the claimed amount a user is entitled to is calculated as <code>userStake</code> * <code>totalLpETH</code>/<code>totalSupply</code>. And as it has been established that <code>totalLpETH</code> was a 1 to 1 exchange, this means that it will be more than <code>totalSupply</code> (since donations had increased <code>address(this).balance</code> but didn't affect <code>totalSupply</code>). As <code>totalLpETH</code> is more than <code>totalSupply</code>, a user's claimed amount will not be in a 1 to 1 ratio with his staked amount, but rather more.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-solidity notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="    function _claim(address _token, address _receiver, uint8 _percentage, Exchange _exchange, bytes calldata _data)
        internal
        returns (uint256 claimedAmount)
    {
        uint256 userStake = balances[msg.sender][_token];
        if (userStake == 0) {
            revert NothingToClaim();
        }
        if (_token == ETH) {
            claimedAmount = userStake.mulDiv(totalLpETH, totalSupply);
            balances[msg.sender][_token] = 0;
            lpETH.safeTransfer(_receiver, claimedAmount);
        }
        ..."><pre>    <span class="pl-k">function<span class="pl-en"> _claim</span></span>(<span class="pl-c1">address</span> <span class="pl-v">_token</span>, <span class="pl-c1">address</span> <span class="pl-v">_receiver</span>, <span class="pl-c1">uint8</span> <span class="pl-v">_percentage</span>, Exchange <span class="pl-v">_exchange</span>, <span class="pl-c1">bytes</span> <span class="pl-k">calldata</span> <span class="pl-v">_data</span>)
        <span class="pl-k">internal</span>
        <span class="pl-k">returns</span> (<span class="pl-c1">uint256</span> <span class="pl-v">claimedAmount</span>)
    {
        <span class="pl-c1">uint256</span> userStake <span class="pl-k">=</span> balances[<span class="pl-c1">msg</span>.<span class="pl-c1">sender</span>][_token];
        <span class="pl-k">if</span> (userStake <span class="pl-k">==</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>) {
            <span class="pl-k">revert</span> <span class="pl-en">NothingToClaim</span>();
        }
        <span class="pl-k">if</span> (_token <span class="pl-k">==</span> ETH) {
            claimedAmount <span class="pl-k">=</span> userStake.<span class="pl-en">mulDiv</span>(totalLpETH, totalSupply);
            balances[<span class="pl-c1">msg</span>.<span class="pl-c1">sender</span>][_token] <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
            lpETH.<span class="pl-en">safeTransfer</span>(_receiver, claimedAmount);
        }
        ...</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">The same also applies if <code>lpETH</code> is donated to the contract before ETH is converted, due to the use of <code>lpETH.balanceOf(address(this));</code> to set <code>totalLpETH</code>.</p>
<p dir="auto">Important to note that this doesn't affect ERC20 stakers, so these donations introduce a disbalance in expected exchange rate of <code>lpETH</code> to <code>ETH</code> and actual exchange rate.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Recommended Mitigation Steps</h3><a id="user-content-recommended-mitigation-steps-1" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Recommended Mitigation Steps" href="#recommended-mitigation-steps-1"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Best way to fix it is to convert only <code>totalSupply</code> of ETH, and setting <code>totalLpETH</code> to <code>totalSupply</code>. That way, the 1 to 1 ratio will be protected. Donations will not be taken into consideration.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-solidity notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="    function convertAllETH() external onlyAuthorized onlyBeforeDate(startClaimDate) {
        if (block.timestamp - loopActivation &lt;= TIMELOCK) {
            revert LoopNotActivated();
        }

        // deposits all the ETH to lpETH contract. Receives lpETH back
        lpETH.deposit{value: totalSupply}(address(this)); //++++

        totalLpETH = totalSupply; //++++ 

        // Claims of lpETH can start immediately after conversion.
        startClaimDate = uint32(block.timestamp);

        emit Converted(totalBalance, totalLpETH);
    }"><pre>    <span class="pl-k">function<span class="pl-en"> convertAllETH</span></span>() <span class="pl-k">external</span> onlyAuthorized <span class="pl-en">onlyBeforeDate</span>(startClaimDate) {
        <span class="pl-k">if</span> (<span class="pl-c1">block</span>.<span class="pl-c1">timestamp</span> <span class="pl-k">-</span> loopActivation <span class="pl-k">&lt;=</span> TIMELOCK) {
            <span class="pl-k">revert</span> <span class="pl-en">LoopNotActivated</span>();
        }

        <span class="pl-c">// deposits all the ETH to lpETH contract. Receives lpETH back</span>
        lpETH.<span class="pl-en">deposit</span>{value: totalSupply}(<span class="pl-c1">address</span>(<span class="pl-mi">this</span>)); <span class="pl-c">//++++</span>

        totalLpETH <span class="pl-k">=</span> totalSupply; <span class="pl-c">//++++ </span>

        <span class="pl-c">// Claims of lpETH can start immediately after conversion.</span>
        startClaimDate <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">uint32</span>(<span class="pl-c1">block</span>.<span class="pl-c1">timestamp</span>);

        <span class="pl-k">emit</span> <span class="pl-en">Converted</span>(totalBalance, totalLpETH);
    }</pre></div>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">3. <code>_claim</code> function can be improved by checking for 0 percentage too.</h2><a id="user-content-3-_claim-function-can-be-improved-by-checking-for-0-percentage-too" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 3. _claim function can be improved by checking for 0 percentage too." href="#3-_claim-function-can-be-improved-by-checking-for-0-percentage-too"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Impact</h3><a id="user-content-impact-2" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Impact" href="#impact-2"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The <a href="https://github.com/code-423n4/2024-05-loop/blob/40167e469edde09969643b6808c57e25d1b9c203/src/PrelaunchPoints.sol#L245">_claim</a> function reverts on 0 user stake to claim. This can be imporved by checking if <code>_percentage</code> is also 0, since it equates to also 0 user claim.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Recommended Mitigation Steps</h3><a id="user-content-recommended-mitigation-steps-2" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Recommended Mitigation Steps" href="#recommended-mitigation-steps-2"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">4. Potential precision loss when claiming</h2><a id="user-content-4-potential-precision-loss-when-claiming" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 4. Potential precision loss when claiming" href="#4-potential-precision-loss-when-claiming"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Impact</h3><a id="user-content-impact-3" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Impact" href="#impact-3"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Depending on how much amount a user had staked, and how much percentage they're willing to claim, users might not be able to claim any token due to precision loss, due to the product of <code>userStake</code> and <code>_percentage</code> being smaller than 100. This is mostly for users with smaller stakes which will not be uncommon, due to the prices of LSTs. Consider scaling up the percentages to handle this potential precision loss.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-solidity notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="        if (_token == ETH) {
            claimedAmount = userStake.mulDiv(totalLpETH, totalSupply);
            balances[msg.sender][_token] = 0;
            lpETH.safeTransfer(_receiver, claimedAmount);
        } else {
            uint256 userClaim = userStake * _percentage / 100;
            _validateData(_token, userClaim, _exchange, _data);
            balances[msg.sender][_token] = userStake - userClaim;"><pre>        <span class="pl-k">if</span> (_token <span class="pl-k">==</span> ETH) {
            claimedAmount <span class="pl-k">=</span> userStake.<span class="pl-en">mulDiv</span>(totalLpETH, totalSupply);
            balances[<span class="pl-c1">msg</span>.<span class="pl-c1">sender</span>][_token] <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
            lpETH.<span class="pl-en">safeTransfer</span>(_receiver, claimedAmount);
        } <span class="pl-k">else</span> {
            <span class="pl-c1">uint256</span> userClaim <span class="pl-k">=</span> userStake <span class="pl-k">*</span> _percentage <span class="pl-k">/</span> <span class="pl-c1">100</span>;
            <span class="pl-en">_validateData</span>(_token, userClaim, _exchange, _data);
            balances[<span class="pl-c1">msg</span>.<span class="pl-c1">sender</span>][_token] <span class="pl-k">=</span> userStake <span class="pl-k">-</span> userClaim;</pre></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">5. Potential transfer to self when claiming and staking <code>ETH</code>/<code>WETH</code>.</h2><a id="user-content-5-potential-transfer-to-self-when-claiming-and-staking-ethweth" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 5. Potential transfer to self when claiming and staking ETH/WETH." href="#5-potential-transfer-to-self-when-claiming-and-staking-ethweth"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Links to affected code *</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/code-423n4/2024-05-loop/blob/0dc8467ccff27230e7c0530b619524cc8401e22a/src/PrelaunchPoints.sol#L230">https://github.com/code-423n4/2024-05-loop/blob/0dc8467ccff27230e7c0530b619524cc8401e22a/src/PrelaunchPoints.sol#L230</a></p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/code-423n4/2024-05-loop/blob/40167e469edde09969643b6808c57e25d1b9c203/src/PrelaunchPoints.sol#L251">https://github.com/code-423n4/2024-05-loop/blob/40167e469edde09969643b6808c57e25d1b9c203/src/PrelaunchPoints.sol#L251</a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Impact</h3><a id="user-content-impact-4" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Impact" href="#impact-4"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">When users with <code>ETH</code>/<code>WETH</code> locks call <code>claimAndStake</code>, the function first claims the users' tokens to the contract (as receiver), before staking on their behalf.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-solidity notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="    function claimAndStake(address _token, uint8 _percentage, Exchange _exchange, bytes calldata _data)
        external
        onlyAfterDate(startClaimDate)
    {
        uint256 claimedAmount = _claim(_token, address(this), _percentage, _exchange, _data);
...
    }"><pre>    <span class="pl-k">function<span class="pl-en"> claimAndStake</span></span>(<span class="pl-c1">address</span> <span class="pl-v">_token</span>, <span class="pl-c1">uint8</span> <span class="pl-v">_percentage</span>, Exchange <span class="pl-v">_exchange</span>, <span class="pl-c1">bytes</span> <span class="pl-k">calldata</span> <span class="pl-v">_data</span>)
        <span class="pl-k">external</span>
        <span class="pl-en">onlyAfterDate</span>(startClaimDate)
    {
        <span class="pl-c1">uint256</span> claimedAmount <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-en">_claim</span>(_token, <span class="pl-c1">address</span>(<span class="pl-mi">this</span>), _percentage, _exchange, _data);
...
    }</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">The <code>_claim</code> function then transfers <code>lpETH</code> (that had existed in the contract upon all <code>ETH</code> conversion) to the receiver, which in this case is address(this) (i.e the contract), introducing a transfer to self situation.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-solidity notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="    function _claim(address _token, address _receiver, uint8 _percentage, Exchange _exchange, bytes calldata _data)
        internal
        returns (uint256 claimedAmount)
    {
...
        if (_token == ETH) {
            claimedAmount = userStake.mulDiv(totalLpETH, totalSupply);
            balances[msg.sender][_token] = 0;
            lpETH.safeTransfer(_receiver, claimedAmount);
        } "><pre>    <span class="pl-k">function<span class="pl-en"> _claim</span></span>(<span class="pl-c1">address</span> <span class="pl-v">_token</span>, <span class="pl-c1">address</span> <span class="pl-v">_receiver</span>, <span class="pl-c1">uint8</span> <span class="pl-v">_percentage</span>, Exchange <span class="pl-v">_exchange</span>, <span class="pl-c1">bytes</span> <span class="pl-k">calldata</span> <span class="pl-v">_data</span>)
        <span class="pl-k">internal</span>
        <span class="pl-k">returns</span> (<span class="pl-c1">uint256</span> <span class="pl-v">claimedAmount</span>)
    {
...
        <span class="pl-k">if</span> (_token <span class="pl-k">==</span> ETH) {
            claimedAmount <span class="pl-k">=</span> userStake.<span class="pl-en">mulDiv</span>(totalLpETH, totalSupply);
            balances[<span class="pl-c1">msg</span>.<span class="pl-c1">sender</span>][_token] <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
            lpETH.<span class="pl-en">safeTransfer</span>(_receiver, claimedAmount);
        } </pre></div>
<p dir="auto">The effects and severity of this is highly dependent on how <code>lpETH</code> is designed to handle transfer to self cases. Some tokens revert on transfer to self, and if <code>lpETH</code> is implemented like that, the <code>claimAndStake</code> function will be virtually unusable for ETH/WETH lockers.
Another possible effect might be accounting issues, if the balanceTo and balanceFrom parameters are cached in its transfer function, and so on.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Recommended Mitigation Steps</h3><a id="user-content-recommended-mitigation-steps-3" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Recommended Mitigation Steps" href="#recommended-mitigation-steps-3"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">It's worth taking into mind when designing the <code>lpETH</code> token.</p>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">6. Ownership can be renounced.</h2><a id="user-content-6-ownership-can-be-renounced" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 6. Ownership can be renounced." href="#6-ownership-can-be-renounced"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Links to affected code *</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/code-423n4/2024-05-loop/blob/0dc8467ccff27230e7c0530b619524cc8401e22a/src/PrelaunchPoints.sol#L336">https://github.com/code-423n4/2024-05-loop/blob/0dc8467ccff27230e7c0530b619524cc8401e22a/src/PrelaunchPoints.sol#L336</a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Impact</h3><a id="user-content-impact-5" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Impact" href="#impact-5"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The <code>setOwner</code> function lacks a zero address check, which causes that the ownership can be renounced. It's especially dangerous if this is done before <code>startClaimDate</code> as users funds will be permanently locked in the protocol.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-solidity notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="    function setOwner(address _owner) external onlyAuthorized {
        owner = _owner;

        emit OwnerUpdated(_owner);
    }"><pre>    <span class="pl-k">function<span class="pl-en"> setOwner</span></span>(<span class="pl-c1">address</span> <span class="pl-v">_owner</span>) <span class="pl-k">external</span> onlyAuthorized {
        owner <span class="pl-k">=</span> _owner;

        <span class="pl-k">emit</span> <span class="pl-en">OwnerUpdated</span>(_owner);
    }</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Recommended Mitigation Steps</h3><a id="user-content-recommended-mitigation-steps-4" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Recommended Mitigation Steps" href="#recommended-mitigation-steps-4"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Best way to fix this is to include a zero address check in the function.
If its desired that ownership can be renounced, to keep the contract fully decentralized, the <code>onlyBeforeDate(startClaimDate)</code> modifier can be added, to prevent renouncing ownership before important protocol functionalities have been completed.</p>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">7. Consider offering a lock with permit function</h2><a id="user-content-7-consider-offering-a-lock-with-permit-function" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 7. Consider offering a lock with permit function" href="#7-consider-offering-a-lock-with-permit-function"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Impact</h3><a id="user-content-impact-6" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Impact" href="#impact-6"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The ERC20 permit functionality is a streamlined, gas efficient and pretty secure way of granting approvals (with limits and deadlines) to spenders. It's become a major feature of many ERC20 tokens and many protocols in the sphere. Some of the tokens supported, e.g <code>pufETH</code>, <code>weETH</code>, offer this functionality. Consider offering a lock with permit function to also take advantage of it.</p>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">8. Some of the tokens in use can be paused which can dos withdrawals, claims and locks</h2><a id="user-content-8-some-of-the-tokens-in-use-can-be-paused-which-can-dos-withdrawals-claims-and-locks" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 8. <div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Impact</h3><a id="user-content-impact-7" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Impact" href="#impact-7"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Rseth, unieth and ezeth can be paused, which temporarily DOSses transfers. This causes that users will not be able to lock their tokens, claim tokens, or withdraw them.</p>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">9. <code>ETH</code> and <code>lpETH</code> deposited after conversion cannot be retrieved, this can be fixed</h2><a id="user-content-9-eth-and-lpeth-deposited-after-conversion-cannot-be-retrieved-this-can-be-fixed" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 9. ETH and lpETH deposited after conversion cannot be retrieved, this can be fixed" href="#9-eth-and-lpeth-deposited-after-conversion-cannot-be-retrieved-this-can-be-fixed"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Links to affected code *</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/code-423n4/2024-05-loop/blob/0dc8467ccff27230e7c0530b619524cc8401e22a/src/PrelaunchPoints.sol#L392">https://github.com/code-423n4/2024-05-loop/blob/0dc8467ccff27230e7c0530b619524cc8401e22a/src/PrelaunchPoints.sol#L392</a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Impact</h3><a id="user-content-impact-8" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Impact" href="#impact-8"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">After the <code>convertAllETH</code> function has been called and all the contract's <code>ETH</code> has been completely converted to lpETH, their respective values are tracked with <code>totalSupply</code> and <code>totalLpETH</code> parameters. Since these cannot be changed any longer after <code>startClaimDate</code>, their values can be used, to determine if excess <code>ETH</code> and <code>lpETH</code> have been sent to the contract, and can be used to retrieve them without disturbing the contracts internal accounting. That way the tokens will not be lost forever.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Recommended Mitigation Steps</h3><a id="user-content-recommended-mitigation-steps-5" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Recommended Mitigation Steps" href="#recommended-mitigation-steps-5"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The function can be a variation of this:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-solidity notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="    function recoverETHorlpETH(address tokenAddress) external onlyAfterDate(startClaimDate) onlyAuthorized {
        if (tokenAddress == address(lpETH)) {
            excessAmount = lpETH.balanceOf(address(this)) - totalLpETH;
            IERC20(tokenAddress).safeTransfer(owner, excessAmount);
        }
        else if (tokenAddress == ETH) {
            excessAmount = address(this).balance - totalSupply;
            (bool sent,) = owner.call{value: excessAmount}(&quot;&quot;); 
            if (!sent) {
                revert FailedToSendEther();
            }
        }
        emit Recovered(tokenAddress, tokenAmount);
    }"><pre>    <span class="pl-k">function<span class="pl-en"> recoverETHorlpETH</span></span>(<span class="pl-c1">address</span> <span class="pl-v">tokenAddress</span>) <span class="pl-k">external</span> <span class="pl-en">onlyAfterDate</span>(startClaimDate) onlyAuthorized {
        <span class="pl-k">if</span> (tokenAddress <span class="pl-k">==</span> <span class="pl-c1">address</span>(lpETH)) {
            excessAmount <span class="pl-k">=</span> lpETH.<span class="pl-en">balanceOf</span>(<span class="pl-c1">address</span>(<span class="pl-mi">this</span>)) <span class="pl-k">-</span> totalLpETH;
            <span class="pl-c1">IERC20</span>(tokenAddress).<span class="pl-en">safeTransfer</span>(owner, excessAmount);
        }
        <span class="pl-k">else</span> <span class="pl-k">if</span> (tokenAddress <span class="pl-k">==</span> ETH) {
            excessAmount <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">address</span>(<span class="pl-mi">this</span>).balance <span class="pl-k">-</span> totalSupply;
            (<span class="pl-c1">bool</span> <span class="pl-v">sent</span>,) <span class="pl-k">=</span> owner.<span class="pl-c1">call</span>{value: excessAmount}(<span class="pl-s">""</span>); 
            <span class="pl-k">if</span> (<span class="pl-k">!</span>sent) {
                <span class="pl-k">revert</span> <span class="pl-en">FailedToSendEther</span>();
            }
        }
        <span class="pl-k">emit</span> <span class="pl-en">Recovered</span>(tokenAddress, tokenAmount);
    }</pre></div>
